CREATE TABLE DBO.DIPENDENTI
(
 COD_DIP             CHAR(6)  NOT NULL
,NOME                VARCHAR(25)  NOT NULL
,INIZIALI            CHAR(2)
,COGNOME             VARCHAR(25)  NOT NULL
,COD_UFF             CHAR(3)
,NUM_TEL_INTERNO     CHAR(4)
,DT_ASSUNZ           DATE
,RUOLO               CHAR(20)
,LIVELLO_ISTRUZIONE  INTEGER
,SESSO               CHAR(1)
,DT_NASCITA          DATE
,STIPENDIO           DECIMAL(9,2)
,BONUS               DECIMAL(9,2)
,COMMISSIONI         DECIMAL(9,2)
);

-- Create Table PROGETTI 
----------------------------------------------------
CREATE TABLE DBO.PROGETTI
(
 COD_PROG                CHAR(6) PRIMARY KEY NOT NULL
,NOME_PROG               VARCHAR(30) NOT NULL
,COD_UFF                 CHAR(3) NOT NULL
,RESPONSABILE            CHAR(6) NOT NULL
,PERC_STAFF_UTILIZZATO   DECIMAL(5,2)
,DT_INI_PROG             DATE
,DT_FIN_PROG             DATE
,PROG_PRINCIPALE         CHAR(6)

----------------------------------------------------
-- Create HR tables
----------------------------------------------------
USE HR
GO

CREATE TABLE DBO.REGIONS  
    ( region_id      INTEGER NOT NULL ,
      region_name    VARCHAR(25));

CREATE TABLE DBO.COUNTRIES 
    ( country_id      CHAR(2) NOT NULL
    , country_name    VARCHAR(40)   
    , region_id INTEGER);

CREATE TABLE DBO.LOCATIONS
    ( location_id    INTEGER   NOT NULL       		        
    , street_address VARCHAR(40)  
    , postal_code    VARCHAR(12)  
    , city           VARCHAR(30)  NOT NULL  
    , state_province VARCHAR(25)  
    , country_id     CHAR(2));

CREATE TABLE DBO.DEPARTMENTS
    ( department_id    INTEGER  NOT NULL 
    , department_name  VARCHAR(30) NOT NULL  
    , manager_id       INTEGER 
    , location_id      INTEGER);

CREATE TABLE DBO.JOBS 
    ( job_id         VARCHAR(10)
    , job_title      VARCHAR(35) NOT NULL
    , min_salary     INTEGER  
    , max_salary     INTEGER);

CREATE TABLE DBO.EMPLOYEES
    ( employee_id    INTEGER
    , first_name     VARCHAR(20)  
    , last_name      VARCHAR(25) NOT NULL  
    , email          VARCHAR(25) NOT NULL  
    , phone_number   VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL
    , hire_date      DATE  NOT NULL
    , job_id         VARCHAR(10) NOT NULL
    , salary         INTEGER NOT NULL CHECK (salary > 0)
    , commission_pct DECIMAL(3,2) 
    , manager_id     INTEGER
    , department_id  INTEGER);

CREATE TABLE DBO.JOB_HISTORY 
    ( employee_id   INTEGER 
    , start_date    DATE NOT NULL
    , end_date      DATE NOT NULL 
    , job_id        VARCHAR(10) NOT NULL  
    , department_id INTEGER);
